There are executive courtesy on the day of check-in. There is afternoon tea in the lounge on the 51st floor of the hotel, with small cakes, cookies, fruits, coffee and tea, and light meals in the evening. The taste is still good, and you can eat enough. It is a warm service.
The swimming pool of the hotel is on the 6th floor. We chose to go before dinner time. There were not many people, and the children had a good time.
The breakfast is on the 1st floor. After reporting the room number, I have to check whether we have breakfast for two. I didn't ask for a long time. In addition, children over 6 years old will be charged 55/person. When there were a lot of people at breakfast, the scene was still a bit chaotic. The cups in the beverage area were all taken out. I saw someone serving coffee in bowls. Haha. Hotels should also be busy and orderly
Finally, I have to say that the service attitude is not good in the reviews. I don‚Äôt know what problems those reviewers encountered and gave bad reviews. Anyway, the waiters we encountered this time were from the lobby, guest room, lounge and restaurant. Very polite, the waiters in the special executive lounge are very friendly and caring
Overall a good stay experience
